MATCH (actor2:Actor {name: 'Harrison Ford'})
MATCH (actor3:Actor {name: 'Carrie Fisher'})
MATCH (actor4:Actor {name: 'Alec Guinness'})
MATCH (dir:Director {name: 'George Lucas'})
MATCH (genreAction:Genre {name: 'Action'})
MATCH (genreAdventure:Genre {name: 'Adventure'})
MATCH (genreFantasy:Genre {name: 'Fantasy'})
MERGE (movie)-[:TEM_GENERO]->(genreAction)
MERGE (movie)-[:TEM_GENERO]->(genreAdventure)
MERGE (movie)-[:TEM_GENERO]->(genreFantasy)
MERGE (actor1)-[:ATUA_EM]->(movie)
MERGE (actor2)-[:ATUA_EM]->(movie)
MERGE (actor3)-[:ATUA_EM]->(movie)
MERGE (actor4)-[:ATUA_EM]->(movie)
MERGE (dir)-[:DIRIGE]->(movie)
